The amenities are well maintained, different swimming pools to choose from, the gym is clean showcases different machines. My room got upgraded, which was very much appreciated! Since I visited during off-season, it was fairly quiet and only a few people were lounging around the pool during the day. The hotel location also allows for a quick stroll along the beachside into the main tourist center. Overall I would definitely recommend the hotel and are genuinely thankful for the hospitality shown to me!

msg:This hotel was nothing short of amazing! GET THE BREAKFAST! The breakfast buffet was everything, the dinner buffet was OK. The hotel has 2 beautiful pools, but you can also swim at the Marriott pools next door as well. Marriott's dinner buffet was very similar but a tad better there. I had the glamorous oceanview room and it was LOVELY. The huge tub in the bathroom was so nice to sit and soak in. My favorite part of the room was the balcony. It was very private and so nice to sit and just look at the beach and the ocean, enjoy a glass or two. It rained a couple of days while I was there so it was nice to sit and listen to the rain. Whenever I was in the room, I opened the balcony door all the way and just relaxed inside. No need to worry about bugs or anything coming into the room. This was probably one of the nicest hotels I have ever stayed in. Also, I can't end this review without raving about the customer service! it was SPLENDID! They did everything I wanted, the came very quickly when I requested for anything. As a foreigner, you almost forget you're in china because of how well they treat you. It was my birthday and they arranged a cake for me and made my bed with special decorations. It was magnificent. I have nothing bad to say about this hotel. If I had to ask for one thing to make my stay better, it would be bottomless mimosas at breakfast. That would have put them over the top. Thanks so much! I would 1000% stay here again. One thing that surprised me was the 10,000 RMB deposit at check in. I prepaid for my room so I wasn't expecting it. I was happy to pay it, but I think it's something they should mention when booking so that customers won't be surprised.
